        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;
        }

          padding: 0;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

          flex-grow: 0;

          padding-right: var(--mr-issue-page-horizontal-padding);

          overflow-y: auto;

          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

          mr-issue-details, mr-launch-overview {

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

The problem was found by my fuzzer, But it cannot be reproduced stably.



<span class="line"><!---->The problem was found by my fuzzer, But it cannot be reproduced stably.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





For some reasons, it does not save the complete asan log, only the path of use.



<span class="line"><!---->For some reasons, it does not save the complete asan log, only the path of use.<!----></span>



<br>





But since it's really a no-interaction UAF inside the gpu process, and I'm not familiar enough with GPUs.



<span class="line"><!---->But since it's really a no-interaction UAF inside the gpu process, and I'm not familiar enough with GPUs.<!----></span>



<br>





So I'm submitting it to you, hoping to help analyze and reproduce the problem. Thanks :)

<div class="issue-diff">
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Status:</strong>
          
          Assigned
          (was: Unconfirmed)
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Owner:</strong>
          
          hcm@google.com
          
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Cc:</strong>
          
          djsollen@google.com scro...@google.com
          
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Labels:</strong>
          
          FoundIn-104 Security_Severity-High OS-Linux OS-Mac OS-Windows Pri-1
          
          <br>
        <!---->
          <strong><!---->Components:</strong>
          
          Blink&gt;WebGL Internals&gt;GPU
          
          <br>
        <!---->
        
      </div>

<br>


    


        


      


        









The POCs do reliably cause the GPU process to terminate on all the platforms I tested (Windows, Linux, Mac). However, I'm unable to reproduce the ASAN crash. As a result, the only indication that this is may security bug is the attached ASAN log indicating UAF in the GPU process, which we'd currently classify as High severity. 



<span class="line"><!---->The POCs do reliably cause the GPU process to terminate on all the platforms I tested (Windows, Linux, Mac). However, I'm unable to reproduce the ASAN crash. As a result, the only indication that this is may security bug is the attached ASAN log indicating UAF in the GPU process, which we'd currently classify as High severity. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





When I tested the POCs on Mac it gave enough log output to indicate that GPU process termination was due to timeout of the watchdog task whilst the GPU process was very busy trying to allocate memory, which would be ImpactNone and WontFix (WAI). 



<span class="line"><!---->When I tested the POCs on Mac it gave enough log output to indicate that GPU process termination was due to timeout of the watchdog task whilst the GPU process was very busy trying to allocate memory, which would be ImpactNone and WontFix (WAI). <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Let's assume this is a security bug for now on the basis that the best path to resolution is to get someone with WebGL experience (and ideally a fresh debugging environment) involved as early as possible.



<span class="line"><!---->Let's assume this is a security bug for now on the basis that the best path to resolution is to get someone with WebGL experience (and ideally a fresh debugging environment) involved as early as possible.<!----></span>
